;export_descr_buildings.txt
; classification option (inside `building` and before first `levels`)
; Example:
;	 classification core|defence|military|trade|water|culture|religious (deprecated, but recognised:fortification|infrastructure|other)
; This tells the game which category of the building browser to use.
; RomeHD has subtly different classifications than the original, so note the deprecated classifications, they wont work anymore.
; If no classification is specified, the game will guess based on the building name, which works for all the unmodded buildings.
; Automatic classification:
;   core_building
;	   core
;   defenses
;	   defence
;   barracks|equestrian|missiles|smith|despotic_law
;	   military
;   market|port_buildings|hinterland_*|caravans
;	   trade
;   health
;	   water
;   academic|amphitheatres|theatres|taverns
;	   culture
;   temple_*|christian_acedemic
;	   religious
; Explicit classification overrides the automatic classification, so if you don't like the above classifications, you can overule them.

;;exclusivity tags, used for the "no_building_tagged" condition
tags
{
	roman
}

;;aliases, give multiple conditions a string (or allow conditions with normally no string to display one)
; alias roman_marian_reforms_triggered
; {
; 	requires factions { roman, } and major_event "marian_reforms"
;
; 	display_string roman_marian_reforms ;;gets a string from expanded_bi
; 	;; if display_string isn't included it will just display the strings for the events normally
; }

alias no_other_roman
{
	requires no_building_tagged roman queued

	display_string SMT_TECH_TREE_THREAD_REQUIRES_ROMAN_DESTRUCTION
}

alias never
{
	requires hidden_resource non_existing_resource

	display_string SMT_BUILDING_TREE_NEVER
}

building core_building
{
    icon government
    levels governors_house governors_villa governors_palace proconsuls_palace imperial_palace
    {
        governors_house requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
                ; To get majority religion in scripts
                upgrade_bodyguard 1 requires majority_religion nubian ;or official_religion?
                upgrade_bodyguard 2 requires majority_religion pagan ;or official_religion?
                upgrade_bodyguard 3 requires majority_religion zoroastrian ;or official_religion?
                upgrade_bodyguard 4 requires majority_religion christianity ;or official_religion?
                ; To counter neighbouring regions' conversion
                religious_belief nubian 1 requires hidden_resource buff_nubian_1
                religious_belief nubian 2 requires hidden_resource buff_nubian_2
                religious_belief nubian 3 requires hidden_resource buff_nubian_3
                religious_belief nubian 4 requires hidden_resource buff_nubian_4
                religious_belief nubian 5 requires hidden_resource buff_nubian_5

;            cost  800
;            settlement_min town
;            upgrades
;            {
;            }
;        }
;    }
;}
building centralizedTree
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels centralized
    {
        centralized requires factions {  all, } and not building_present decentralizedTree
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            faction_capability
            {
                construction_cost_bonus_religious bonus 10
                construction_cost_bonus_military bonus 10
                construction_cost_bonus_other bonus 10
                taxable_income_bonus bonus 10
                happiness_bonus bonus -2
                law_bonus bonus -2
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
}
building decentralizedTree
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels decentralized
    {
        decentralized requires factions {  all, } and not building_present centralizedTree
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            faction_capability
            {
                happiness_bonus bonus 2
                law_bonus bonus 2
                extra_construction_points bonus 1
                construction_cost_bonus_religious bonus -10
                construction_cost_bonus_military bonus -10
                construction_cost_bonus_other bonus -10
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -10
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
}

;; Governance mode
;; autonomous_region     fast   | . happiness | . law | .morale | --income | 0 troops    |  0 building options
;; province              medium | --happiness | --law | .morale | -income | some troops | all building options
;; integrated_terittory  slow   | - happiness | - law | +morale | income | all troops  | all building options, [culture > 60%]
building province_governance_mode
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels governance_mode autonomous_region province integrated_terittory
    {
        governance_mode requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min village
            upgrades
            {
                autonomous_region
                province
                integrated_terittory
            }
        }
        autonomous_region requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -20
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        province requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -10
                happiness_bonus bonus -2
                law_bonus bonus -2
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        integrated_terittory requires factions { all, } and religion nubian >= 60
        {
            capability
            {
                happiness_bonus bonus -1
                law_bonus bonus -1
                recruits_morale_bonus bonus 1
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
}

; Economic Policies
; Exploitation -pop | -happiness | -law | -trade | .building_time | +income | -morale
; Balanced     .pop | .happiness | .law | .trade | .building_time | .income | .morale
; Development  +pop | +happiness | +law | +trade | +building_time | -income | +morale
building province_economical_policy
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels economical_policy development balanced exploitation
    {
        economical_policy requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min village
            upgrades
            {
                development
                balanced
                exploitation
            }
        }
        development requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
                population_growth_bonus bonus 1
                happiness_bonus bonus 2
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus 2
                extra_construction_points bonus 1
                recruits_morale_bonus bonus 1
                law_bonus bonus -1
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1000
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        balanced requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        exploitation requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
                population_growth_bonus bonus -1
                happiness_bonus bonus -2
                law_bonus bonus -2
                trade_base_income_bonus bonus -2
                recruits_morale_bonus bonus -1
                taxable_income_bonus bonus 100
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
}
; Cultural Policies
; Tolerant     . religious_belief | . happiness | . law | .income                    [g>province]
; Integration  + religious_belief | - happiness | - law | +income                    [g>province]
; Assimilation ++religious_belief | --happiness | --law | -income                    [g>province]
building province_cultural_policy
{
    classification core
    icon government
    levels cultural_policy tolerant integration assimilation
    {
        cultural_policy requires factions { all, }
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min village
            upgrades
            {
                tolerant
                integration
                assimilation
            }
        }
        tolerant requires factions { all, } and building_present_min_level province_governance_mode province or building_present_min_level province_governance_mode integrated_terittory
        {
            capability
            {
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        integration requires factions { all, } and building_present_min_level province_governance_mode province or building_present_min_level province_governance_mode integrated_terittory
        {
            capability
            {
                taxable_income_bonus bonus 10
                religious_belief nubian 1
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 90
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 60
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 30
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 90
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 60
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 30
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
        assimilation requires factions { all, } and building_present_min_level province_governance_mode province or building_present_min_level province_governance_mode integrated_terittory
        {
            capability
            {
                religious_belief nubian 2
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 90
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 80
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 70
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 60
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 50
                happiness_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 40
                happiness_bonus bonus -2 requires religion nubian < 30
                happiness_bonus bonus -2 requires religion nubian < 20
                happiness_bonus bonus -3 requires religion nubian < 10
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 90
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 80
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 70
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 60
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 50
                law_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 40
                law_bonus bonus -2 requires religion nubian < 30
                law_bonus bonus -2 requires religion nubian < 20
                law_bonus bonus -3 requires religion nubian < 10
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 90
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 80
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 70
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 60
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 50
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 40
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 30
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 20
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -1 requires religion nubian < 10
            }
            construction  1
            cost  800
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
            }
        }
    }
}

; Problem: Religion difference unrest by default
; Solution: Change religions' unrest factor to 0

; Problem: Culture unrest is calculated based on buildings of foreign culture
; Solution: Give all buildings to all cultures (requires factions), but restrict building with religion requirement.

building defenses
{
    icon defense
    levels wooden_pallisade wooden_wall stone_wall large_stone_wall epic_stone_wall
    {
        wooden_pallisade requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, nubia, }
        {
            capability
            {
                wall_level 0
                tower_level 1
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -6
                happiness_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
            } 
            construction  1
            cost  1200
            settlement_min town
            upgrades
            {
                wooden_wall
            } 
        } 
        wooden_wall requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, nubia, }
        {
            capability
            {
                wall_level 1
                gate_strength 1
                tower_level 1
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -12
                happiness_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
            } 
            construction  2
            cost  2400
            settlement_min large_town
            upgrades
            {
                stone_wall
            } 
        } 
        stone_wall requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, nubia, }
        {
            capability
            {
                wall_level 2
                tower_level 1
                gate_defences 1
                gate_strength 1
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -18
                happiness_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
                law_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
            } 
            construction  3
            cost  4800
            settlement_min city
            upgrades
            {
                large_stone_wall
            } 
        } 
        large_stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } 
        {
            capability
            {
                wall_level 3
                tower_level 1
                gate_defences 2
                gate_strength 2
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -24
                happiness_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
                law_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
            } 
            construction  5
            cost  8000
            settlement_min large_city
            upgrades
            {
                epic_stone_wall
            } 
        } 
        epic_stone_wall requires factions { carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } 
        {
            capability
            {
                wall_level 4
                tower_level 2
                gate_defences 2
                gate_strength 2
                taxable_income_bonus bonus -30
                happiness_bonus bonus 1 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
                law_bonus bonus 2 requires factions { barbarian, nomad, carthaginian, eastern, parthia, egypt, greek, roman, } and remastered_only
            } 
            construction  6
            cost  18000
            settlement_min huge_city
            upgrades
            {
            } 
        } 
    } 
    plugins
    {
    } 
} 
building barracks
{
    icon infantry
